<Date>1528175383165< /Date>< Review>
Abysmal. I have pretty low standard for pho, but what I got from Mumfresh can not be classified as Pho. To start off, the portion is about a third of a standard bowl of pho, and the price is almost double that. As to be somewhat expected at an airport, if this was the only problem, this review would be much higher.

Their "beef broth" I'm pretty sure is the hot water they pour into the bowl to cook the rare steak, and therefore has a slight tinge of flavor. I never thought anything with cilantro, onions, shallots, and scallions could possible be tasteless, yet it is almost as if they did not season their food in the slightest way. The highlight of the meal, was when I ate a single slice of raw onion by itself. Their condiments come in small packets located behind the counter, rather than the multiple bottles they have on their shelves. Apparently used purely for appearances. I would advise asking for a lot of condiments, you'll need it to actually taste anything.

Service itself was pretty mediocre, took a while to get serviced, and even longer for them to call out my food was ready. Between the time they finished my food, and called out my number, the "rare steak" had already gone well done.

Overall, this experience was one that left my mouth with a bad taste of no taste at all, and a small hole in my wallet. Highly recommend people to avoid this place, I'm still hungry.</Review>

<Rate>5</Rate><user>117919405724463655222</user>< Review>
Mono Cup is the best stop along 395 for good coffee, they simply know how to do Coffee, Espresso drinks and the other drinks you'd expect at a dedicated coffee house...perfectly. they also offer light pastry and snack fare, breakfast sandwiches and bottled drinks for sale.  The prices are great, and considering the coffee, the value is off the charts. My wife thinks they have the best white chocolate mocha she's ever had, I love their house medium roast, and have also had their coldbrew (best I've ever had)...the service is excellent...the line was out the door the other day and reinforcments arrived quickly...always a smile and friendly goodbye. ..they truly care about doing it right and making you happy!

Update: summer 2018....it is as great as ever...if you are looking for coffee near Lee Vining...it's at Mono Cup!</Review>

<user_name>CHRISTINA COLEMAN< /user_name>< review>
The RVs are pretty dated, absolutely nothing fancy, including no GPS and no bluetooth stereo.  The black water sensor never worked, and the LP detector malfunctioned and started beeping on our first night, requiring that we take the RV to a repair shop to have it disconnected, and we had to buy a plug in one to use in the meantime.  Later, the check engine light went on for no apparent reason.  But the customer service was phenomenal.  When we had issues with the above, we called the 800 number and get help right away.  Cruise America paid for the repair directly and reimbursed us for one day's rental fee for our inconvenience, in addition to reimbursing us for the plug-in.  The RV worked well the rest of the trip, which was just over 1800 miles, and our family of 4 fared well in the small but very functional space.  We would use them again.<//review>

<time>1624376490310</time><Rating>4< /Rating><review>The RVs are pretty dated, absolutely nothing fancy, including no GPS and no bluetooth stereo.  The black water sensor never worked, and the LP detector malfunctioned and started beeping on our first night, requiring that we take the RV to a repair shop to have it disconnected, and we had to buy a plug in one to use in the meantime.  Later, the check engine light went on for no apparent reason.  But the customer service was phenomenal.  When we had issues with the above, we called the 800 number and get help right away. <text>My 3rd time renting from Cruise America. Each time the RV has worked great and the check-in/out experience was good. The first 2 rentals were from the LAX/Carson facility.

This time we rented from the Downey location and although the door sign read masks required, none of the staff had masks on. I was a bit disappointed in their lack of adherence to the guidelines.

We got to our campsite the first night and the next morning I noticed the rear passenger tire looked low - bought a gauge and the tire was definitely low ~20psi. I put some air in it and watched it for the next 3 days - seemed like a slow leak. I decided to have it fixed while we were staying in one location for a couple days. Turns out there was a screw in the tire.  Given the slow leak, I‚Äôm pretty sure it was in the tire when we picked it up and the folks in the Downey office hadn‚Äôt checked the tire pressure.

I did submit the expense and there was no question about refunding me the amount. I think we were lucky we did t get a flat on the road with the pressure so low.

The other disappointing part of the check-out was that the staff didn‚Äôt run through the vehicle with me. They asked if I had rented before and when the answer was yes, they assumed that I knew everything about how to operate the RV - which was true, but then I was left to check all of the items such as making sure the generator worked, the stove would light, etc.

Overall, the experience with Cruise America was good and I‚Äôll definitely rent from them again.< /text>< username>

< text>
This is the best Mongolian grill type of restaurant I‚Äôve ever been to! You pick all of your ingredients and then they cook it in front of you. I got mine to go and was very pleased with the amount of food for the price! For around $13 I got a big bowl of my custom stir fry, hot and sour pork soup (which was delicious), rice, and wontons with sweet and sour dipping sauce. Usually when I go to these types of grills my food loses a lot of the sauce and I‚Äôm left wishing I had more, not the case!!! My noodles were not dry and had amazing flavor. I was also surprised that they had lamb as a meat option! I would like to see some seafood on the line, but I was still very impressed. The atmosphere was nice and clean. Every employee was kind and personal, even the cooks. AWESOME JOB HULA!< /text>

Chico's famous Mongolian BBQ. You select from tons of fresh meats, fresh veggies, tofu, noodles and sauces and at the end of the line it's stir fried on a huge grill while you watch. < text>
Very adequate Mongolian BBQ, but nowhere near the best I've been to. I don't get the people raving about it being the best. If you are just a casual Mongolian BBQ customer, you may well love it. However, for the more discerning Mongolian BBQ fan, there are much better places. Maybe not in Chico, so perhaps it's the best in the immediate vicinity. The sauces and oils could be better with more traditional options added. Good selection of meats. Staff was friendly, and the cooks worked hard, kept the grill moving, and cleaned it when it had been used a lot. Would I eat there again? Sure, if I were in the area. Would I write home about it? Not really. Not bad at all, but far from the hype I read and heard about.<//text>

<user_id>100349278881960011084</user_id>< username>
Chris Logue< /username>
<date>1473036981230<//date><rating>5</rating>< text>
Fantastic food, fair price.

Hula's has two locations in the Chico area, though there's little to distinguish the two aside from the 20th street location being slightly larger. Both locations are home to the best (and until recently, only) Mongolian barbecue in Butte county .

Now, Chico is a college town, so one must come prepared for the possibility of encountering some liberally-minded college snowflakes; at times this place can be utterly packed, meaning standing in a line of up to an hour on some occasions, but I can't hold the establishment's clientele or popularity against them.

All in all, it's worth the price and worth the patience. Fill your first bowl to the brim, eat what you can, and take the rest home!<//text>

We do have pineapple as a topping if you would like to add fruit to your bowls in the future. While we appreciate you making a long journey to dine at Hula's, I'm sorry to hear if your last visit did not live up to your expectations. I hope this helps in your understanding of our system and welcome you back for another meal again soon. Take care!"}<//Resp>
